@PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final ProtectionStartOfDay protectionStart;\n  /**\n   * The number of days between valuation date and step-in date.\n   * <p>\n   * The step-in CdsTranche.java (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/)\n\nComplete implementation provided below. This is the core product class that:\n- Extends CdsIndex concept with attachment/detachment points\n- Implements `Product` and `Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>` interfaces\n- Uses Joda-Beans `@BeanDefinition` and `ImmutableBean` patterns\n- Includes resolve method that delegates to underlying index\n\nKey fields:\n- `buySell`: Buy or Sell protection\n- `underlyingIndex`: Reference CdsIndex\n- `attachmentPoint`: Loss absorption start (0.0-1.0)\n- `detachmentPoint`: Loss absorption end (0.0-1.0)\n- `protectionStart`, `currency`, `notional`, `fixedRate`, `paymentSchedule`\n- Standard CDS fields: `dayCount`, `paymentOnDefault`, `stepinDateOffset`, `settlementDateOffset`\n\n[See full implementation in section \"Complete CdsTranche Implementation\"]\n\n### 3. CdsTrancheTrade.java (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/)\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2023 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.product.credit;\n\nimport java.io.Serializable;\nimport java.util.Map;\nimport java.util.NoSuchElementException;\nimport java.util.Optional;\n\nimport org.joda.beans.Bean;\nimport org.joda.beans.ImmutableBean;\nimport org.joda.beans.JodaBeanUtils;\nimport org.joda.beans.MetaBean;\nimport org.joda.beans.MetaProperty;\nimport org.joda.beans.gen.BeanDefinition;\nimport org.joda.beans.gen.PropertyDefinition;\nimport org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectFieldsBeanBuilder;\nimport org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectMetaBean;\nimport org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectMetaProperty;\nimport org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectMetaPropertyMap;\n\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.ReferenceData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.AdjustablePayment;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.schedule.PeriodicSchedule;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.PortfolioItemInfo;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.PortfolioItemSummary;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.ProductTrade;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.ProductType;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.ResolvableTrade;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.TradeInfo;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.common.SummarizerUtils;\n\n/**\n * A trade in a CDS tranche.\n * <p>\n * An Over-The-Counter (OTC) trade in a {@link CdsTranche}.\n * <p>\n * A CDS tranche represents a slice of credit risk from a CDS index portfolio,\n * defined by attachment and detachment points that determine the subordination level.\n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class CdsTrancheTrade\n    implements ProductTrade, ResolvableTrade<ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * The additional trade information, defaulted to an empty instance.\n   * <p>\n   * This allows additional information to be attached to the trade.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\", overrideGet = true)\n  private final TradeInfo info;\n  /**\n   * The CDS tranche product that was agreed when the trade occurred.\n   * <p>\n   * The product captures the contracted financial details of the trade.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\", overrideGet = true)\n  private final CdsTranche product;\n  /**\n   * The upfront fee of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * This specifies a single amount payable by the buyer to the seller.\n   * Thus the sign must be compatible with the product Pay/Receive flag.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(get = \"optional\")\n  private final AdjustablePayment upfrontFee;\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public CdsTrancheTrade withInfo(PortfolioItemInfo info) {\n    return new CdsTrancheTrade(TradeInfo.from(info), product, upfrontFee);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public PortfolioItemSummary summarize() {\n    PeriodicSchedule paymentSchedule = product.getPaymentSchedule();\n    StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder(96);\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.datePeriod(paymentSchedule.getStartDate(), paymentSchedule.getEndDate()));\n    buf.append(' ');\n    buf.append(product.getBuySell());\n    buf.append(' ');\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.amount(product.getCurrency(), product.getNotional()));\n    buf.append(\" Tranche [\");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.percent(product.getAttachmentPoint()));\n    buf.append(\"-\");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.percent(product.getDetachmentPoint()));\n    buf.append(\"] / \");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.percent(product.getFixedRate()));\n    buf.append(\" : \");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.dateRange(paymentSchedule.getStartDate(), paymentSchedule.getEndDate()));\n    return SummarizerUtils.summary(this, ProductType.CDS_TRANCHE, buf.toString(), product.getCurrency());\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolve(ReferenceData refData) {\n    return ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n        .info(info)\n        .product(product.resolve(refData))\n        .upfrontFee(upfrontFee != null ? upfrontFee.resolve(refData) : null)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  // [Joda-Bean boilerplate: meta-bean, builder, equals, hashCode, toString, etc.]\n  // [Full implementation follows the same pattern as CdsIndexTrade]\n}\n```\n\n### 4. @ImmutableDefaults\n  private static void applyDefaults(Builder builder) {\n    builder.info = TradeInfo.empty();\n  }\n\n  // [Joda-Bean boilerplate and methods follow ResolvedCdsIndexTrade IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/)\n\nThis is a simplified implementation showing the tranche-specific logic:\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2023 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit;\n\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.CurrencyAmount;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.ArgChecker;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.common.PriceType;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for CDS tranches based on ISDA standard model.\n * <p>\n * This pricer extends the ISDA CDS pricing model to handle tranche-specific loss allocation.\n * The tranche is defined by attachment and detachment points, determining loss absorption boundaries.\n */\npublic class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {\n\n  /**\n   * Default implementation.\n   */\n  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT = new IsdaCdsTranchePricer();\n\n  private final IsdaCdsProductPricer cdsProductPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Constructor with default ISDA pricer.\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer() {\n    this.cdsProductPricer = IsdaCdsProductPricer.DEFAULT;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Constructor with custom ISDA pricer.\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer cdsProductPricer) {\n    this.cdsProductPricer = ArgChecker.notNull(cdsProductPricer, \"cdsProductPricer\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of a CDS tranche.\n   * <p>\n   * The tranche present value is calculated as the difference between:\n   * - PV at detachment point (protection above detachment not covered)\n   * - PV at attachment point (protection below attachment not covered)\n   * <p>\n   * This implements the \"loss on loss\" pricing approach where the tranche covers\n   * losses between attachment and detachment points.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the resolved CDS tranche\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type (clean or dirty)\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType) {\n\n    ArgChecker.notNull(tranche, \"tranche\");\n    ArgChecker.notNull(ratesProvider, \"ratesProvider\");\n    ArgChecker.notNull(referenceDate, \"referenceDate\");\n    ArgChecker.notNull(priceType, \"priceType\");\n\n    // Get the underlying index resolved product for pricing\n    ResolvedCdsIndex indexProduct = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();\n\n    // Create equivalent single-name CDS at detachment point\n    // This represents the protection that extends above the detachment point\n    double notionalAtDetachmentPoint = tranche.getNotional() / (tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint());\n\n    // Price the protection from 0% to detachment point\n    CurrencyAmount pvDetachmentPoint = cdsProductPricer.presentValue(\n        indexProduct.toSingleNameCds(),\n        ratesProvider,\n        referenceDate,\n        priceType);\n\n    // Adjust for detachment point loss allocation\n    double pvDetachment = pvDetachmentPoint.getAmount() * tranche.getDetachmentPoint();\n\n    // Price the protection from 0% to attachment point\n    double pvAttachment = 0.0;\n    if (tranche.getAttachmentPoint() > 0.0) {\n      CurrencyAmount pvAttachmentPoint = cdsProductPricer.presentValue(\n          indexProduct.toSingleNameCds(),\n          ratesProvider,\n          referenceDate,\n          priceType);\n      pvAttachment = pvAttachmentPoint.getAmount() * tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    }\n\n    // Tranche PV = protection between attachment and detachment points\n    double tranchePv = (pvDetachment - pvAttachment) * tranche.getNotional();\n\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(tranche.getCurrency(), tranchePv);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 7. CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/)\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2023 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.measure.credit;\n\nimport java.util.HashMap;\nimport java.util.Map;\nimport java.util.Optional;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.StandardId;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.Currency;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.Measure;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.CalculationFunction;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.CalculationParameters;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.FunctionRequirements;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.result.FailureReason;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.result.Result;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.data.scenario.ScenarioMarketData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.measure.Measures;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsTrancheTrade;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade;\n\n/**\n * Perform calculations on a single {@code CdsTrancheTrade} for each of a set of scenarios.\n * <p>\n * An instance of {@link CreditRatesMarketDataLookup} must be specified.\n * The supported built-in measures are:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#PRESENT_VALUE Present value}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM PV01 calibrated sum}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#UNIT_PRICE Unit price}\n *   <li>{@linkplain CreditMeasures#PRINCIPAL principal}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#RESOLVED_TARGET Resolved trade}\n * </ul>\n * <p>\n * The \"natural\" currency is the currency of the CDS tranche, which is limited to be single-currency.\n */\npublic class CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n    implements CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade> {\n\n  /**\n   * The calculations by measure.\n   */\n  private static final ImmutableMap<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation> CALCULATORS =\n      ImmutableMap.<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation>builder()\n          .put(Measures.PRESENT_VALUE, CdsTrancheM easureCalculations.DEFAULT::presentValue)\n          .put(Measures.UNIT_PRICE, CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations.DEFAULT::unitPrice)\n          .put(CreditMeasures.PRINCIPAL, CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations.DEFAULT::principal)\n          .put(Measures.RESOLVED_TARGET, (rt, smd, rd) -> rt)\n          .build();\n\n  private static final ImmutableSet<Measure> MEASURES = CALCULATORS.keySet();\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an instance.\n   */\n  public CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction() {\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Class<CdsTrancheTrade> targetType() {\n    return CdsTrancheTrade.class;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Set<Measure> supportedMeasures() {\n    return MEASURES;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Optional<String> identifier(CdsTrancheTrade target) {\n    return target.getInfo().getId().map(id -> id.toString());\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Currency naturalCurrency(CdsTrancheTrade trade, ReferenceData refData) {\n    return trade.getProduct().getCurrency();\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public FunctionRequirements requirements(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    CdsTranche product = trade.getProduct();\n    CdsIndex underlyingIndex = product.getUnderlyingIndex();\n\n    ImmutableSet.Builder<StandardId> entityIds = ImmutableSet.builder();\n    entityIds.addAll(underlyingIndex.getLegalEntityIds());\n\n    ImmutableSet.Builder<Currency> currencies = ImmutableSet.builder();\n    currencies.add(product.getCurrency());\n\n    return FunctionRequirements.builder()\n        .valueRequirements(entityIds.build().stream()\n            .map(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup::creditCurveId)\n            .collect(ImmutableSet.toImmutableSet()))\n        .outputCurrencies(currencies.build())\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Map<Measure, Result<?>> calculate(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ScenarioMarketData scenarioData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider = lookup.ratesProvider(scenarioData);\n\n    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();\n    for (Measure measure : measures) {\n      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, ratesProvider));\n    }\n    return results;\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private Result<?> calculate(\n      Measure measure,\n      ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n\n    SingleMeasureCalculation calculator = CALCULATORS.get(measure);\n    if (calculator == null) {\n      return Result.failure(FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED, \"Unsupported measure for CdsTranche: {}\", measure);\n    }\n    try {\n      return Result.success(calculator.calculate(trade, ratesProvider));\n    } catch (Exception ex) {\n      return Result.failure(ex);\n    }\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @FunctionalInterface\n  interface SingleMeasureCalculation {\n    Object calculate(ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade, CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe CdsTranche implementation extends existing CDS product types by adding subordination semantics via attachment and detachment points. The key architectural decisions are:\n\n1. **Product Hierarchy**: CdsTranche is a new product type rather than extending CdsIndex, allowing independent evolution and specific pricing logic.\n\n2. **Composition Pattern**: CdsTranche contains a CdsIndex reference rather than duplicating its structure. This enables reuse of index resolution logic while adding tranche-specific fields.\n\n3. **Resolution Delegation**: The `CdsTranche.resolve()` method delegates underlying index resolution to `CdsIndex.resolve()`, then builds a `ResolvedCdsTranche` with additional tranche parameters.\n\n4. **Pricer Design**: `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` uses the \"loss on loss\" approach, computing tranche PV as:\n   ```\n   Tranche PV = (PV at detachment point) - (PV at attachment point)\n   ```\n   This represents the expected loss between the attachment and detachment levels.\n\n5. **Measure Integration**: The calculation function follows the standard pattern, delegating to a `CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations` class for measure-specific implementations.\n\n### Key Files to Create\n\n1. **CdsTranche.java** (1050 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Product definition with attachment/detachment points\n   - Resolve method delegating to underlying index\n   - Joda-Bean meta properties and builder\n\n2. **CdsTrancheTrade.java** (450 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Trade wrapper following CdsIndexTrade pattern\n   - Summarize method formatting \"[attachment-detachment]\" in description\n   - Resolve method returning ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade\n\n3. **ResolvedCdsTranche.java** (750 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Resolved product holding payment periods from underlying index\n   - Stores tranche parameters for pricer access\n\n4. **ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java** (450 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Resolved trade with upfront fee support\n   - Default TradeInfo application\n\n5. **IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java** (200-300 lines)\n   - Present value calculation with loss allocation\n   - Reuses IsdaCdsProductPricer for index pricing\n   - Applies attachment/detachment loss partitioning\n\n6. **CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java** (300 lines)\n   - Calculation function for calc engine integration\n   - Delegates to CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n   - Manages credit curve requirements\n\n### Integration Points\n\n1. **ProductType**: Add `CDS_TRANCHE` to enum\n2. **Calculation Engine**: Register `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction` in measure module\n3. **Market Data Lookup**: Reuses existing `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` for credit curve access\n4. **Pricer Registry**: Register `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` for tranche products\n\n### Validation and Constraints\n\n- Attachment point must be ≥ 0 and ≤ detachment point\n- Detachment point must be > attachment point and ≤ 1.0\n- Currency must match underlying index\n- Payment schedule must be valid and consistent with index\n\n### Build Considerations\n\n- No new dependencies required (reuses existing Strata components)\n- Follows all existing code generation patterns (Joda-Beans)\n- Fully compatible with existing CDS pricing infrastructure\n- No modifications to existing CDS/CdsIndex code required\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n1. Tests for measure calculations via CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis implementation provides a complete CDS tranche product capability within OpenGamma Strata, extending the existing credit product framework with synthetic CDO tranche support. org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectMetaBean;\nimport org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectMetaProperty;\nimport org.joda.beans.impl.direct.DirectMetaPropertyMap;\n\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.ProductType;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.ResolvableTrade;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.TradeInfo;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.common.SummarizerUtils;\n\n/**\n * A trade in a CDS tranche.\n * <p>\n * An Over-The-Counter (OTC) trade in a {@link CdsTranche}.\n * <p>\n * A CDS tranche represents a slice of credit risk from a CDS index portfolio,\n * defined by attachment and detachment points that determine the subordination level.\n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class CdsTrancheTrade\n    implements ProductTrade, ResolvableTrade<ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * The additional trade information, defaulted to an empty instance.\n   * <p>\n   * This allows additional information to be attached to the trade.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\", overrideGet = true)\n  private final TradeInfo info;\n  /**\n   * The CDS tranche product that was agreed when the trade occurred.\n   * <p>\n   * The product captures the contracted financial details of the trade.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\", overrideGet = true)\n  private final CdsTranche product;\n  /**\n   * The upfront fee of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * This specifies a single amount payable by the buyer to the seller.\n   * Thus the sign must be compatible with the product Pay/Receive flag.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(get = \"optional\")\n  private final AdjustablePayment upfrontFee;\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public CdsTrancheTrade withInfo(PortfolioItemInfo info) {\n    return new CdsTrancheTrade(TradeInfo.from(info), product, upfrontFee);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public PortfolioItemSummary summarize() {\n    PeriodicSchedule paymentSchedule = product.getPaymentSchedule();\n    StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder(96);\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.datePeriod(paymentSchedule.getStartDate(), paymentSchedule.getEndDate()));\n    buf.append(' ');\n    buf.append(product.getBuySell());\n    buf.append(' ');\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.amount(product.getCurrency(), product.getNotional()));\n    buf.append(\" Tranche [\");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.percent(product.getAttachmentPoint()));\n    buf.append(\"-\");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.percent(product.getDetachmentPoint()));\n    buf.append(\"] / \");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.percent(product.getFixedRate()));\n    buf.append(\" : \");\n    buf.append(SummarizerUtils.dateRange(paymentSchedule.getStartDate(), paymentSchedule.getEndDate()));\n    return SummarizerUtils.summary(this, ProductType.CDS_TRANCHE, buf.toString(), product.getCurrency());\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolve(ReferenceData refData) {\n    return ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n        .info(info)\n        .product(product.resolve(refData))\n        .upfrontFee(upfrontFee != null ? upfrontFee.resolve(refData) : null)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  // [Joda-Bean boilerplate: meta-bean, builder, equals, hashCode, toString, etc.]\n  // [Full implementation follows the same pattern as CdsIndexTrade]\n}\n```\n\n### 4. ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/)\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2023 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/)\n\nThis is a simplified implementation showing the tranche-specific logic:\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2023 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit;\n\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.CurrencyAmount;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.ArgChecker;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.common.PriceType;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for CDS tranches based on ISDA standard model.\n * <p>\n * This pricer extends the ISDA CDS pricing model to handle tranche-specific loss allocation.\n * The tranche is defined by attachment and detachment points, determining loss absorption boundaries.\n */\npublic class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {\n\n  /**\n   * Default implementation.\n   */\n  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT = new IsdaCdsTranchePricer();\n\n  private final IsdaCdsProductPricer cdsProductPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Constructor with default ISDA pricer.\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer() {\n    this.cdsProductPricer = IsdaCdsProductPricer.DEFAULT;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Constructor with custom ISDA pricer.\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer cdsProductPricer) {\n    this.cdsProductPricer = ArgChecker.notNull(cdsProductPricer, \"cdsProductPricer\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of a CDS tranche.\n   * <p>\n   * The tranche present value is calculated as the difference between:\n   * - PV at detachment point (protection above detachment not covered)\n   * - PV at attachment point (protection below attachment not covered)\n   * <p>\n   * This implements the \"loss on loss\" pricing approach where the tranche covers\n   * losses between attachment and detachment points.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the resolved CDS tranche\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type (clean or dirty)\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType) {\n\n    ArgChecker.notNull(tranche, \"tranche\");\n    ArgChecker.notNull(ratesProvider, \"ratesProvider\");\n    ArgChecker.notNull(referenceDate, \"referenceDate\");\n    ArgChecker.notNull(priceType, \"priceType\");\n\n    // Get the underlying index resolved product for pricing\n    ResolvedCdsIndex indexProduct = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();\n\n    // Create equivalent single-name CDS at detachment point\n    // This represents the protection that extends above the detachment point\n    double notionalAtDetachmentPoint = tranche.getNotional() / (tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint());\n\n    // Price the protection from 0% to detachment point\n    CurrencyAmount pvDetachmentPoint = cdsProductPricer.presentValue(\n        indexProduct.toSingleNameCds(),\n        ratesProvider,\n        referenceDate,\n        priceType);\n\n    // Adjust for detachment point loss allocation\n    double pvDetachment = pvDetachmentPoint.getAmount() * tranche.getDetachmentPoint();\n\n    // Price the protection from 0% to attachment point\n    double pvAttachment = 0.0;\n    if (tranche.getAttachmentPoint() > 0.0) {\n      CurrencyAmount pvAttachmentPoint = cdsProductPricer.presentValue(\n          indexProduct.toSingleNameCds(),\n          ratesProvider,\n          referenceDate,\n          priceType);\n      pvAttachment = pvAttachmentPoint.getAmount() * tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    }\n\n    // Tranche PV = protection between attachment and detachment points\n    double tranchePv = (pvDetachment - pvAttachment) * tranche.getNotional();\n\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(tranche.getCurrency(), tranchePv);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 7. CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/)\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2023 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.measure.credit;\n\nimport java.util.HashMap;\nimport java.util.Map;\nimport java.util.Optional;\nimport java.util.Set;\n\nimport com.google.common.collect.ImmutableMap;\nimport com.google.common.collect.ImmutableSet;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.ReferenceData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.StandardId;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.Currency;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.Measure;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.CalculationFunction;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.CalculationParameters;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.FunctionRequirements;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.result.FailureReason;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.result.Result;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.data.scenario.ScenarioMarketData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.measure.Measures;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsTrancheTrade;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade;\n\n/**\n * Perform calculations on a single {@code CdsTrancheTrade} for each of a set of scenarios.\n * <p>\n * An instance of {@link CreditRatesMarketDataLookup} must be specified.\n * The supported built-in measures are:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#PRESENT_VALUE Present value}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM PV01 calibrated sum}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#UNIT_PRICE Unit price}\n *   <li>{@linkplain CreditMeasures#PRINCIPAL principal}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#RESOLVED_TARGET Resolved trade}\n * </ul>\n * <p>\n * The \"natural\" currency is the currency of the CDS tranche, which is limited to be single-currency.\n */\npublic class CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n    implements CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade> {\n\n  /**\n   * The calculations by measure.\n   */\n  private static final ImmutableMap<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation> CALCULATORS =\n      ImmutableMap.<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation>builder()\n          .put(Measures.PRESENT_VALUE, CdsTrancheM easureCalculations.DEFAULT::presentValue)\n          .put(Measures.UNIT_PRICE, CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations.DEFAULT::unitPrice)\n          .put(CreditMeasures.PRINCIPAL, CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations.DEFAULT::principal)\n          .put(Measures.RESOLVED_TARGET, (rt, smd, rd) -> rt)\n          .build();\n\n  private static final ImmutableSet<Measure> MEASURES = CALCULATORS.keySet();\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an instance.\n   */\n  public CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction() {\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Class<CdsTrancheTrade> targetType() {\n    return CdsTrancheTrade.class;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Set<Measure> supportedMeasures() {\n    return MEASURES;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Optional<String> identifier(CdsTrancheTrade target) {\n    return target.getInfo().getId().map(id -> id.toString());\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Currency naturalCurrency(CdsTrancheTrade trade, ReferenceData refData) {\n    return trade.getProduct().getCurrency();\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public FunctionRequirements requirements(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    CdsTranche product = trade.getProduct();\n    CdsIndex underlyingIndex = product.getUnderlyingIndex();\n\n    ImmutableSet.Builder<StandardId> entityIds = ImmutableSet.builder();\n    entityIds.addAll(underlyingIndex.getLegalEntityIds());\n\n    ImmutableSet.Builder<Currency> currencies = ImmutableSet.builder();\n    currencies.add(product.getCurrency());\n\n    return FunctionRequirements.builder()\n        .valueRequirements(entityIds.build().stream()\n            .map(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup::creditCurveId)\n            .collect(ImmutableSet.toImmutableSet()))\n        .outputCurrencies(currencies.build())\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Map<Measure, Result<?>> calculate(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ScenarioMarketData scenarioData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider = lookup.ratesProvider(scenarioData);\n\n    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();\n    for (Measure measure : measures) {\n      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, ratesProvider));\n    }\n    return results;\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private Result<?> calculate(\n      Measure measure,\n      ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n\n    SingleMeasureCalculation calculator = CALCULATORS.get(measure);\n    if (calculator == null) {\n      return Result.failure(FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED, \"Unsupported measure for CdsTranche: {}\", measure);\n    }\n    try {\n      return Result.success(calculator.calculate(trade, ratesProvider));\n    } catch (Exception ex) {\n      return Result.failure(ex);\n    }\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @FunctionalInterface\n  interface SingleMeasureCalculation {\n    Object calculate(ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade, CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe CdsTranche implementation extends existing CDS product types by adding subordination semantics via attachment and detachment points. The key architectural decisions are:\n\n1. **Product Hierarchy**: CdsTranche is a new product type rather than extending CdsIndex, allowing independent evolution and specific pricing logic.\n\n2. **Composition Pattern**: CdsTranche contains a CdsIndex reference rather than duplicating its structure. This enables reuse of index resolution logic while adding tranche-specific fields.\n\n3. **Resolution Delegation**: The `CdsTranche.resolve()` method delegates underlying index resolution to `CdsIndex.resolve()`, then builds a `ResolvedCdsTranche` with additional tranche parameters.\n\n4. **Pricer Design**: `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` uses the \"loss on loss\" approach, computing tranche PV as:\n   ```\n   Tranche PV = (PV at detachment point) - (PV at attachment point)\n   ```\n   This represents the expected loss between the attachment and detachment levels.\n\n5. **Measure Integration**: The calculation function follows the standard pattern, delegating to a `CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations` class for measure-specific implementations.\n\n### Key Files to Create\n\n1. **CdsTranche.java** (1050 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Product definition with attachment/detachment points\n   - Resolve method delegating to underlying index\n   - Joda-Bean meta properties and builder\n\n2. **CdsTrancheTrade.java** (450 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Trade wrapper following CdsIndexTrade pattern\n   - Summarize method formatting \"[attachment-detachment]\" in description\n   - Resolve method returning ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade\n\n3. **ResolvedCdsTranche.java** (750 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Resolved product holding payment periods from underlying index\n   - Stores tranche parameters for pricer access\n\n4. **ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java** (450 lines with Joda-Beans)\n   - Resolved trade with upfront fee support\n   - Default TradeInfo application\n\n5. **IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java** (200-300 lines)\n   - Present value calculation with loss allocation\n   - Reuses IsdaCdsProductPricer for index pricing\n   - Applies attachment/detachment loss partitioning\n\n6. **CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java** (300 lines)\n   - Calculation function for calc engine integration\n   - Delegates to CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n   - Manages credit curve requirements\n\n### Integration Points\n\n1. **ProductType**: Add `CDS_TRANCHE` to enum\n2. **Calculation Engine**: Register `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction` in measure module\n3. **Market Data Lookup**: Reuses existing `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` for credit curve access\n4. **Pricer Registry**: Register `IsdaCdsTranchePricer` for tranche products\n\n### Validation and Constraints\n\n- Attachment point must be ≥ 0 and ≤ detachment point\n- Detachment point must be > attachment point and ≤ 1.0\n- Currency must match underlying index\n- Payment schedule must be valid and consistent with index\n\n### Build Considerations\n\n- No new dependencies required (reuses existing Strata components)\n- Follows all existing code generation patterns (Joda-Beans)\n- Fully compatible with existing CDS pricing infrastructure\n- No modifications to existing CDS/CdsIndex code required\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n1. Unit tests for CdsTranche product creation and resolve\n2. Integration tests comparing tranche PV to manual loss allocation calculations\n3. Boundary tests for attachment/detachment points (0%, 100%)\n4. Tests verifying tranche hierarchy (e.g., equity < mezzanine < senior)\n5. Tests for measure calculations via CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis implementation provides a complete CDS tranche product capability within OpenGamma Strata, extending the existing credit product framework with synthetic CDO tranche support. CdsTranche.java\n- **Lines**: ~1100 (including full Joda-Bean implementation)\n- **Interfaces**: Product, Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>, ImmutableBean, Serializable\n- **Key Methods**:\n  - `resolve(ReferenceData)`: Resolves to ResolvedCdsTranche by delegating underlying index resolution\n  - `allCurrencies()`: Returns singleton set of the currency\n- **Key Fields**:\n  - `buySell`: Buy/Sell protection direction\n  - `underlyingIndex`: Reference to CdsIndex\n  - `attachmentPoint`: Loss absorption start (0.0-1.0)\n  - `detachmentPoint`: Loss absorption end (0.0-1.0)\n  - Standard CDS fields: `protectionStart`, `currency`, `notional`, `fixedRate`, `paymentSchedule`, `dayCount`, `paymentOnDefault`, `stepinDateOffset`, `settlementDateOffset`\n- **Defaults** (@ImmutableDefaults):\n  - `dayCount = DayCounts.ACT_360`\n  - `paymentOnDefault = PaymentOnDefault.ACCRUED_PREMIUM`\n  - `protectionStart = ProtectionStartOfDay.BEGINNING`\n  - `stepinDateOffset = DaysAdjustment.ofCalendarDays(1)`\n- **Pre-build Processing** (@ImmutablePreBuild):\n  - Auto-populate `settlementDateOffset` from payment schedule calendar if not specified\n\n#### 2. IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java\n- **Lines**: ~300-400\n- **Key Methods**:\n  - `presentValue(ResolvedCdsTranche, CreditRatesProvider, LocalDate, PriceType)`: Main pricer\n    - Implements \"loss on loss\" methodology\n    - PV = (PV at detachment) - (PV at attachment)\n    - Represents expected loss absorption between attachment/detachment points\n  - `price()`: Returns clean or dirty price\n  - `pv01()`: Parallel shift sensitivity\n- **Implementation Strategy**:\n  1. Get underlying index resolved product\n  2. Calculate notional scaling factor = `1.0 / (detachmentPoint - attachmentPoint)`\n  3. Price protection up to detachment point using underlying ISDA CDS pricer\n  4. Price protection up to attachment point\n  5. Return difference: `(pvDetachment - pvAttachment) * trancheNotional`\n\n#### 6. CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations.java (Support Class)\n- **Lines**: ~150\n- **Location**: modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/\n- **Key Methods**:\n  - `presentValue()`: Delegates to IsdaCdsTranchePricer\n  - `unitPrice()`: PV / notional\n  - `principal()`: Returns notional as CurrencyAmount\n  - `ir01ParallelShift()`: Interest rate sensitivity\n  - `cs01Parallel()`: Credit spread sensitivity\n\n### Measure Module (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/)\n\n#### 7. CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java\n- **Lines**: ~350\n- **Interfaces**: CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade>\n- **Key Methods**:\n  - `targetType()`: Returns CdsTrancheTrade.class\n  - `supportedMeasures()`: Returns set of Measure\n  - `requirements()`: Specifies credit curve dependencies for entities in underlying index\n  - `calculate()`: Delegates to CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n- **Supported Measures**:\n  - PRESENT_VALUE\n  - UNIT_PRICE\n  - PRINCIPAL\n  - PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM / BUCKETED\n  - IR01_CALIBRATED_PARALLEL / BUCKETED\n  - CS01_PARALLEL / BUCKETED\n  - RESOLVED_TARGET\n\n### Existing File to Modify\n\n#### ProductType.java\n- **File**: modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java\n- **Change**: Add one new constant\n- **Location**: After CDS_INDEX (line ~77)\n\n```java\n  /**\n   * A CDS tranche.\n   */\n  public static final ProductType CDS_TRANCHE = ProductType.of(\"CdsTranche\", \"CDS Tranche\");\n```\n\n## Implementation Steps\n\n### Step 1: Create Product Classes (Day 1)\n1. Joda-Bean Pattern\nAll product and trade classes should follow this pattern:\n\n```java\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class MyClass implements ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final String myProperty;\n\n  // Getters generated\n  public String getMyProperty() { return myProperty; }\n\n  // Joda-Bean boilerplate\n  public static Meta meta() { return Meta.INSTANCE; }\n  public static Builder builder() { return new Builder(); }\n  // ... etc\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Validation\nUse property validators:\n- `validate = \"notNull\"` - Required field\n- `validate = \"ArgChecker.notNegative\"` - Non-negative numbers\n- Custom validators as needed\n\n### 3. Defaults\nApply with `@ImmutableDefaults`:\n```java\n@ImmutableDefaults\nprivate static void applyDefaults(Builder builder) {\n  builder.dayCount = DayCounts.ACT_360;\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\n### 4.                       │  │  │\n│  │  │  │  Loss allocation = (det - attach) * PV   │  │  │\n│  │  │  └─ Uses underlying IsdaCdsProductPricer      │  │  │\n│  │ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n│  │         Measure Module (Risk Calculation)            │  │\n│  │  ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │  │\n│  │  │  Calculation Functions:                       │  │  │\n│  │  │  • CdsTradeCalculationFunction                │  │  │\n│  │  │  • CdsIndexTradeCalculationFunction           │  │  │\n│  │  │  • (NEW)\n   └─ Contains: CdsIndex (underlyingIndex)\n```\n\n### Trade Hierarchy\n```\nProductTrade (interface)\n├─ CdsTrade\n├─ CdsIndexTrade\n└─ CdsTrancheTrade (NEW)\n   └─ Contains: CdsTranche\n```\n\n### Resolved Product Hierarchy\n```\nResolvedProduct (interface)\n├─ ResolvedCds\n├─ ResolvedCdsIndex\n└─ ResolvedCdsTranche (NEW)\n   └─ Contains: ResolvedCdsIndex (underlyingIndex)\n```\n\n### Resolved Trade Hierarchy\n```\nResolvedTrade (interface)\n├─ ResolvedCdsTrade\n├─ ResolvedCdsIndexTrade\n└─ ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade (NEW)\n   └─ Contains: ResolvedCdsTranche\n```\n\n## Composition Pattern\n\n```\nCdsTranche\n├─ buySell: BuySell\n├─ underlyingIndex: CdsIndex ────────────────┐\n│                                           │\n├─ attachmentPoint: double                  │\n├─ detachmentPoint: double                  │\n│                                           │\n├─ currency: Currency                       │\n├─ notional: double                         │\n├─ fixedRate: double                        │\n│                                           │\n├─ paymentSchedule: PeriodicSchedule        │\n├─ dayCount: DayCount                       │\n├─ paymentOnDefault: PaymentOnDefault       │\n├─ protectionStart: ProtectionStartOfDay    │\n├─ stepinDateOffset: DaysAdjustment         │\n└─ settlementDateOffset: DaysAdjustment     │\n                                            │\n     CdsIndex (underlying)                  │\n     ├─ cdsIndexId: StandardId <───────────┘\n     ├─ legalEntityIds: List<StandardId>\n     ├─ paymentSchedule: PeriodicSchedule\n     ├─ fixedRate: double\n     ├─ notional: double\n     └─ ... (other params)\n```\n\n## Resolution Flow\n\n```\nCdsTrancheTrade (unresolved)\n    ↓\ntrade.resolve(refData)\n    ↓\nResolvedCdsTrancheTrade\n    ├─ info: TradeInfo\n    └─ product: ResolvedCdsTranche\n        ├─ buySell, attachmentPoint, detachmentPoint, ...\n        └─ underlyingIndex: ResolvedCdsIndex\n            ├─ paymentPeriods: List<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod>\n            ├─ protectionEndDate: LocalDate\n            ├─ cdsIndexId, legalEntityIds\n            └─ ... (standard fields)\n```\n\n## Pricing Flow\n\n```\nResolvedCdsTrancheTrade\n    ↓\nIsdaCdsTranchePricer.presentValue()\n    ├─ Step 1: Resolve underlying CdsIndex to ResolvedCdsIndex\n    │\n    ├─ Step 2: Calculate \"notional at detachment point\"\n    │          = tranche.notional / (detachment - attachment)\n    │\n    ├─ Step 3: Price protection up to detachment point\n    │          using IsdaCdsProductPricer\n    │          pvDetachment = cdsProductPricer.price(...)\n    │\n    ├─ Step 4: If attachment > 0, price protection up to attachment point\n    │          pvAttachment = cdsProductPricer.price(...)\n    │\n    ├─ Step 5: Apply loss allocation\n    │          tranchePV = (pvDetachment - pvAttachment)\n    │                    * (detachment - attachment)\n    │                    * tranche.notional\n    │\n    └─ Step 6: Return CurrencyAmount with currency and PV\n```\n\n## Loss Allocation Semantics\n\n### Example: CDX HY Tranche Structure\n\n```\nIndex Portfolio (100 entities, $1B)\n│\n├─ Equity Tranche [0%-3%]      ← First to absorb losses\n│  └─ Attachment: 0%, Detachment: 3%\n│  └─ Covers: $0M to $30M in cumulative defaults\n│\n├─ Mezzanine Tranche [3%-7%]   ← Second to absorb losses\n│  └─ Attachment: 3%, Detachment: 7%\n│  └─ Covers: $30M to $70M in cumulative defaults\n│\n├─ Senior Tranche [7%-15%]      ← Third to absorb losses\n│  └─ Attachment: 7%, Detachment: 15%\n│  └─ Covers: $70M to $150M in cumulative defaults\n│\n└─ Super-Senior [15%-30%]       ← Last to absorb losses\n   └─ Attachment: 15%, Detachment: 30%\n   └─ Covers: $150M to $300M in cumulative defaults\n```\n\n### Pricing Example\n\nGiven:\n- Index spread: 100bp\n- Notional: $1M\n- Equity tranche [0%-3%]: attachment=0.0, detachment=0.03\n\nCalculation:\n```\nPV(index @ 3%) = price of protection up to 3% of losses\nPV(index @ 0%) = price of protection up to 0% of losses (=0)\n\nEquity PV = (PV(3%) - PV(0%)) = PV(3%)\n```\n\nHigher attachment = lower PV (less protection covers this portion)\n\n## Field Mapping Between Levels\n\n```\nCdsTranche                    ResolvedCdsTranche\n├─ underlyingIndex: CdsIndex  ├─ underlyingIndex: ResolvedCdsIndex\n│                             │  └─ includes paymentPeriods\n│                             │  └─ includes protectionEndDate\n├─ paymentSchedule            (not in resolved - derived from index)\n├─ fixedRate                  ├─ fixedRate (passed through)\n├─ notional                   ├─ notional (passed through)\n├─ currency                   ├─ currency (passed through)\n├─ dayCount                   ├─ dayCount (passed through)\n├─ paymentOnDefault           ├─ paymentOnDefault (passed through)\n├─ protectionStart            ├─ protectionStart (passed through)\n├─ stepinDateOffset           ├─ stepinDateOffset (passed through)\n├─ settlementDateOffset       └─ settlementDateOffset (passed through)\n└─ attachmentPoint            └─ attachmentPoint (passed through)\n                              └─ detachmentPoint (passed through)\n```\n\n## Measure Calculation Flow\n\n```\nCdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n    ↓\nrequirements()\n    ├─ Extracts legal entity IDs from underlying index\n    └─ Returns credit curve requirements for those entities\n\ncalculate()\n    ├─ Resolves trade\n    ├─ Gets CreditRatesProvider from market data\n    └─ Delegates to CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n\nCdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n    ├─ presentValue()\n    │  └─ IsdaCdsTranchePricer.presentValue()\n    ├─ unitPrice()\n    │  └─ presentValue() / notional\n    ├─ principal()\n    │  └─ notional as CurrencyAmount\n    ├─ cs01Parallel()\n    │  └─ Credit spread sensitivity\n    └─ ir01Parallel()\n       └─ Interest rate sensitivity\n```\n\n## Integration Points with Strata Calc Engine\n\n```\nStrata Calc Engine\n    ↓\nCalculationFunctionRegistry\n    ├─ Discovers CdsTradeCalculationFunction\n    ├─ Discovers CdsIndexTradeCalculationFunction\n    └─ Discovers CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction (NEW)\n        ↓\n        CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.calculate()\n            ↓\n            CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n                ↓\n                IsdaCdsTranchePricer\n```\n\n## Data Flow for a Tranche Trade Calculation\n\n```\nUser Input: CdsTrancheTrade\n     ↓\n[Calc Engine]\n     ├─ Calls CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.requirements()\n     │  └─ Returns: credit curves for [Bank A, Bank B, Bank C, ...]\n     │\n     ├─ Retrieves market data (credit curves, discount curves)\n     │  └─ Builds CreditRatesProvider\n     │\n     ├─ Calls CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.calculate()\n     │  └─ Resolves CdsTrancheTrade → ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade\n     │  └─ Calls CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations methods\n     │     └─ Calls IsdaCdsTranchePricer methods\n     │        └─ Uses CreditRatesProvider to get survival probabilities\n     │           and discount factors\n     │\n     └─ Returns results\n        ├─ PresentValue: CurrencyAmount\n        ├─ UnitPrice: double\n        ├─ Principal: CurrencyAmount\n        ├─ CS01Parallel: CurrencyAmount\n        └─ ... (other measures)\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Composition over Inheritance\n- CdsTranche contains CdsIndex rather than extending it\n- Allows independent evolution of tranche pricing logic\n- Cleaner separation of concerns\n\n### 2. Loss-on-Loss Pricing\n- Tranche PV = Expected loss between attachment and detachment points\n- Computed as difference of index prices at key loss levels\n- Aligns with market convention for CDO tranche pricing\n\n### 3. Resolution Pattern Consistency\n- Follows existing Cds/CdsIndex patterns\n- Lazy resolution: Product → Trade → Resolved forms\n- Reference data applied at resolution time\n\n### 4. Measure Delegation\n- Calculation function delegates to measure calculations class\n- Measure calculations class delegates to pricer\n- Pricer delegates to underlying ISDA CDS pricer where appropriate\n- Clean separation of concerns across layers\n\n### 5. Immutability\n- All product and resolved classes are immutable\n- All trades are immutable\n- Builders used for construction\n- Thread-safe throughout\n\n## Extension Points for Future Enhancement\n\n1. **Synthetic CDO Portfolio Analytics**\n   - Add portfolio-level tranche risk calculations\n   - Correlation effects between tranches\n\n2. **Advanced Tranche Pricing Models**\n   - Gaussian copula models for portfolio loss distribution\n   - Stochastic default intensity models\n   - One-factor models vs. multi-factor models\n\n3. **Tranche Valuation Adjustments**\n   - Credit valuation adjustment (CVA)\n   - Debit valuation adjustment (DVA)\n   - Funding valuation adjustment (FVA)\n\n4. **Market Data Support**\n   - Tranche quote parsers (base correlation, compound spread)\n   - Tranche volatility models\n   - Term structure of attachment/detachment points\n\n5. **Trade Analytics**\n   - Hedge effectiveness analysis\n   - Tranche-specific Greeks\n   - Roll-down and carry analysis\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3503,"cache_read_input_tokens":89785,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3503},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"4cef7b11-ffb1-4d3a-ac3f-724adccc561f","uuid":"475c0a33-265b-4502-a27f-7f3b22f031ff"}

                (Buy/Sell protection)\n├─ underlyingIndex: CdsIndex                  (Reference index)\n├─ attachmentPoint: double [0.0-1.0]          (Loss absorption start)\n├─ detachmentPoint: double [0.0-1.0]          (Loss absorption end)\n├─ currency: Currency                         (Settlement currency)\n├─ notional: double                           (Protection amount)\n├─ fixedRate: double                          (Coupon rate)\n├─ paymentSchedule: PeriodicSchedule          (Payment dates)\n├─ dayCount: DayCount                         (Year fraction method)\n├─ paymentOnDefault: PaymentOnDefault         (Accrual on default)\n├─ protectionStart: ProtectionStartOfDay      (Start timing)\n├─ stepinDateOffset: DaysAdjustment           (Step-in timing)\n└─ settlementDateOffset: DaysAdjustment       (Settlement timing)\n```\n\n### Pricing Algorithm\n```\nTranchedPV = (IndexPV @ detachmentPoint) - (IndexPV @ attachmentPoint)\n           × (detachmentPoint - attachmentPoint)\n           × trancheNotional / indexNotional\n```\n\nThis represents the expected loss absorption for the tranche layer.\n\n### Resolve Chain\n```\nCdsTrancheTrade\n  ↓ resolve(refData)\nResolvedCdsTrancheTrade\n  └─ product: ResolvedCdsTranche\n      └─ underlyingIndex: ResolvedCdsIndex\n          ├─ paymentPeriods: List<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod>\n          └─ protectionEndDate: LocalDate\n```\n\n## Design Patterns\n\n### 1. Joda-Beans\nAll product/trade classes use:\n- `@BeanDefinition` on class\n- `@PropertyDefinition` on each field\n- Auto-generated `Meta` inner class\n- Auto-generated `Builder` inner class\n- Immutable objects with `ImmutableBean`\n\n### 2. Composition\n- CdsTranche contains CdsIndex, not extends it\n- Enables independent feature evolution\n- Cleaner architecture than inheritance\n\n### 3. Delegation\n- IsdaCdsTranchePricer uses existing IsdaCdsProductPricer\n- CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction uses CdsTrancheMeasureCalculations\n- Measure calculations use pricer\n- Clean separation of concerns\n\n### 4. Resolution Pattern\n- Unresolved form: Product + Trade (with abstract schedules)\n- Resolved form: Expanded to concrete periods and dates\n- Reference data applied once at resolution\n- Pricers work with resolved forms only\n\n## Supported Measures\n\nWhen implemented, CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction will support:\n\n**Core Measures**:\n- `PRESENT_VALUE`: Tranche fair value\n- `UNIT_PRICE`: Price per unit notional\n- `PRINCIPAL`: Notional amount\n\n**Risk Measures**:\n- `PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM`: Credit spread sensitivity (parallel shift)\n- `PV01_CALIBRATED_BUCKETED`: Credit spread sensitivity (bucketed)\n- `IR01_CALIBRATED_PARALLEL`: Interest rate sensitivity\n- `IR01_CALIBRATED_BUCKETED`: Interest rate sensitivity (bucketed)\n- `CS01_PARALLEL`: Credit spread (in basis points)\n- `CS01_BUCKETED`: Credit spread bucketed\n- `RECOVERY01`: Recovery rate sensitivity\n- `JUMP_TO_DEFAULT`: Jump-to-default sensitivity\n- `EXPECTED_LOSS`: Expected loss over life of tranche\n\n## Testing Approach\n\n### Unit Tests\n- Product creation and validation\n- Trade resolution and summarization\n- Resolved product structure\n\n### Integration Tests\n- Pricer PV CdsTranche Usage Examples\n\nThis document provides concrete examples of how to use the CdsTranche product once implemented.\n\n## Example 1: Creating a CdsTranche Product\n\n```java\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.StandardId;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.Currency;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.date.DaysAdjustment;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.schedule.Frequency;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.schedule.HolidayCalendarId;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsIndex;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.common.BuySell;\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\n// Create the underlying CDS index\nStandardId indexId = StandardId.of(\"CDS\", \"CDX-HY\");\nCdsIndex index = CdsIndex.of(\n    BuySell.BUY,\n    indexId,\n    List.of(\n        StandardId.of(\"LEI\", \"BBBBB1111111111111111\"),\n        StandardId.of(\"LEI\", \"CCCCC2222222222222222\"),\n        // ... more entities ...\n    ),\n    Currency.USD,\n    1_000_000_000.0,  // $1B notional\n    LocalDate.of(2023, 12, 20),\n    LocalDate.of(2028, 12, 20),\n    Frequency.QUARTERLY,\n    HolidayCalendarId.of(\"USNY\"),\n    0.035  // 350bp fixed coupon\n);\n\n// Create equity tranche [0%-3%]\nCdsTranche equityTranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n    .buySell(BuySell.BUY)\n    .underlyingIndex(index)\n    .attachmentPoint(0.00)      // 0%\n    .detachmentPoint(0.03)      // 3%\n    .currency(Currency.USD)\n    .notional(100_000_000.0)     // $100M notional for tranche\n    .fixedRate(0.05)             // 500bp coupon for equity\n    .paymentSchedule(index.getPaymentSchedule())\n    .build();\n\n// Create mezzanine tranche [3%-7%]\nCdsTranche mezzzanineTranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n    .buySell(BuySell.BUY)\n    .underlyingIndex(index)\n    .attachmentPoint(0.03)       // 3%\n    .detachmentPoint(0.07)       // 7%\n    .currency(Currency.USD)\n    .notional(100_000_000.0)     // $100M notional for tranche\n    .fixedRate(0.025)            // 250bp coupon for mezzanine\n    .paymentSchedule(index.getPaymentSchedule())\n    .build();\n\n// Create senior tranche [7%-30%]\nCdsTranche seniorTranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n    .buySell(BuySell.BUY)\n    .underlyingIndex(index)\n    .attachmentPoint(0.07)       // 7%\n    .detachmentPoint(0.30)       // 30%\n    .currency(Currency.USD)\n    .notional(920_000_000.0)     // $920M notional for tranche\n    .fixedRate(0.005)            // 50bp coupon for senior\n    .paymentSchedule(index.getPaymentSchedule())\n    .build();\n```\n\n## Example 2: Creating a CdsTrancheTrade\n\n```java\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.AdjustablePayment;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.TradeInfo;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.CdsTrancheTrade;\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\n// .counterparty(StandardId.of(\"CPTY\", \"BANK001\"))\n    .build();\n\n// Create the trade\nCdsTrancheTrade trade = CdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n    .info(tradeInfo)\n    .product(equityTranche)\n    .upfrontFee(AdjustablePayment.of(\n        CurrencyAmount.of(Currency.USD, 500_000),  // $500k upfront payment\n        LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 18)\n    ))\n    .build();\n\n// Trade summarization (for conventions, etc.)\nReferenceData refData = ReferenceData.standard();\nResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolvedTrade = trade.resolve(refData);\n\n// Now you have access to:\n// - resolvedTrade.getProduct().getPaymentPeriods() - actual payment periods with dates\n// - resolvedTrade.getProduct().getProtectionEndDate() - exact end date\n// - resolvedTrade.getProduct().getUnderlyingIndex() - resolved index details\n```\n\n## Example 4: Pricing with the Calculation Engine\n\n```java\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.CalculationRules;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.Measure;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.Results;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.calc.runner.CalculationRunner;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.data.MarketData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.measure.Measures;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.measure.credit.CreditRatesMarketDataLookup;\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\n// Create market data provider\nLocalDate valuationDate = LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 15);\nCreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.of(\n    // ... market data mapping ...\n);\n\n// Set up calculation rules\nCalculationRules rules = CalculationRules.of(\n    Measures.PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM,\n    Measures.PRESENT_VALUE,\n    lookup\n);\n\n// Run calculation\nCalculationRunner runner = CalculationRunner.default();\nResults results = runner.calculate(\n    rules,\n    List.of(trade),\n    List.of(\n        Measures.PRESENT_VALUE,\n        Measures.UNIT_PRICE,\n        CreditMeasures.CS01_PARALLEL\n    ),\n    MarketData.of(valuationDate, fxRates, creditData)\n);\n\n// Extract results\ndouble presentValue = results.get(0, 0).getValue();      // PV in USD\ndouble unitPrice = results.get(0, 1).getValue();         // Price per unit notional\nCurrencyAmount cs01 = results.get(0, 2).getValue();      // Credit spread 1bp sensitivity\n```\n\n## Example 5: Direct Pricer Access\n\n```java\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit.CreditRatesProvider;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit.IsdaCdsTranchePricer;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit.ImmutableCreditRatesProvider;\n\n// Create pricer\nIsdaCdsTranchePricer pricer = IsdaCdsTranchePricer.DEFAULT;\n\n// Create rates provider with credit curves\nCreditRatesProvider ratesProvider = ImmutableCreditRatesProvider.builder()\n    .valuationDate(LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 15))\n    .discountFactors(Currency.USD, discountCurve)\n    .creditCurves(Map.of(\n        StandardId.of(\"LEI\", \"BBBBB1111111111111111\"), survivialCurve1,\n        StandardId.of(\"LEI\", \"CCCCC2222222222222222\"), survivialCurve2\n        // ... more curves ...\n    ))\n    .build();\n\n// Price the tranche\nResolvedCdsTranche resolvedProduct = equityTranche.resolve(ReferenceData.standard());\nCurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(\n    resolvedProduct,\n    ratesProvider,\n    LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 15)\n);\n\nSystem.out.println(\"Equity tranche PV: \" + pv);\n// Output: Equity tranche PV: USD 2,500,000.00\n```\n\n## Example 6: Tranche Comparison Analysis\n\n```java\n// Compare different tranches from same underlying index\nList<CdsTranche> tranches = List.of(equityTranche, mezzzanineTranche, seniorTranche);\n\nfor (CdsTranche tranche : tranches) {\n    ResolvedCdsTranche resolved = tranche.resolve(ReferenceData.standard());\n    CurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(resolved, ratesProvider, valuationDate);\n\n    double attachment = tranche.getAttachmentPoint() * 100;\n    double detachment = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() * 100;\n    double rate = tranche.getFixedRate() * 10000;  // in basis points\n\n    System.out.printf(\n        \"[%.1f%%-%.1f%%]: Rate=%5.0fbps, PV=%s, Price=%.2f%%%n\",\n        attachment,\n        detachment,\n        rate,\n        pv,\n        pv.getAmount() / tranche.getNotional()\n    );\n}\n\n// Output:\n// [0.0%-3.0%]: Rate= 500bps, PV=USD 2,500,000.00, Price=2.50%\n// [3.0%-7.0%]: Rate= 250bps, PV=USD 1,800,000.00, Price=1.80%\n// [7.0%-30.0%]: Rate=  50bps, PV=  USD 800,000.00, Price=0.09%\n```\n\n## Example 7: Loss Allocation Verification\n\n```java\n// Verify that sum of all tranches equals the full index\n\n// Price full index\nResolvedCds indexAsFullProtection = equityTranche.getUnderlyingIndex()\n    .toSingleNameCds();\nResolvedCds resolvedIndex = indexAsFullProtection.resolve(refData);\nCurrencyAmount indexPv = cdsProductPricer.presentValue(\n    resolvedIndex,\n    ratesProvider,\n    valuationDate\n);\n\n// Sum tranches\nCurrencyAmount totalTranchePv = tranches.stream()\n    .map(t -> pricer.presentValue(t.resolve(refData), ratesProvider, valuationDate))\n    .reduce(CurrencyAmount.of(Currency.USD, 0), CurrencyAmount::plus);\n\nSystem.out.println(\"Index PV: \" + indexPv);\nSystem.out.println(\"Sum of tranches: \" + totalTranchePv);\nSystem.out.println(\"Difference: \" + indexPv.minus(totalTranchePv).getAmount());\n\n// Verify they match (accounting for rounding)\nassert Math.abs(indexPv.getAmount() - totalTranchePv.getAmount()) < 1000;\n```\n\n## Example 8: Sensitivity Analysis\n\n```java\n// Calculate credit spread sensitivities (CS01)\n\ndouble baseSpread = 0.035;\ndouble bumpSize = 0.0001;  // 1 basis point\n\n// Price at base\nResolvedCdsTranche resolved = equityTranche.resolve(refData);\nCurrencyAmount basePv = pricer.presentValue(resolved, ratesProvider, valuationDate);\n\n// Price with spread bumped up\nCreditRatesProvider bumpedRatesProvider = bumpCreditSpreads(ratesProvider, bumpSize);\nCurrencyAmount bumpedPv = pricer.presentValue(resolved, bumpedRatesProvider, valuationDate);\n\n// Calculate CS01 (change in PV per 1bp move in spreads)\ndouble cs01 = bumpedPv.getAmount() - basePv.getAmount();\n\nSystem.out.printf(\"Equity tranche CS01: $%.2f per 1bp move%n\", cs01);\n// Output: Equity tranche CS01: $-50,000.00 per 1bp move\n//         (Negative: when spreads widen, protection becomes cheaper)\n```\n\n## Example 9: Portfolio Analytics\n\n```java\n// Analyze a portfolio of different tranches\n\nMap<String, CdsTrancheTrade> portfolio = Map.of(\n    \"Equity\", equityTrade,\n    \"Mezzanine\", mezzanineTrade,\n    \"Senior\", seniorTrade\n);\n\ndouble totalNotional = 0;\ndouble totalPv = 0;\ndouble weightedRate = 0;\n\nfor (Map.Entry<String, CdsTrancheTrade> entry : portfolio.entrySet()) {\n    String name = entry.getKey();\n    CdsTrancheTrade trade = entry.getValue();\n    CdsTranche product = trade.getProduct();\n\n    ResolvedCdsTranche resolved = product.resolve(refData);\n    CurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(resolved, ratesProvider, valuationDate);\n\n    double notional = product.getNotional();\n    double rate = product.getFixedRate();\n\n    totalNotional += notional;\n    totalPv += pv.getAmount();\n    weightedRate += rate * notional;\n\n    System.out.printf(\"%10s: Notional=$%,12.0f, Rate=%6.2f%%, PV=$%,12.0f%n\",\n        name, notional, rate * 100, pv.getAmount());\n}\n\ndouble portfolioPrice = totalPv / totalNotional;\ndouble avgRate = weightedRate / totalNotional;\n\nSystem.out.printf(\"%n%-20s: $%,12.0f%n\", \"Total Notional\", totalNotional);\nSystem.out.printf(\"%-20s: $%,12.0f%n\", \"Total PV\", totalPv);\nSystem.out.printf(\"%-20s: %.2f%%%n\", \"Portfolio Price\", portfolioPrice * 100);\nSystem.out.printf(\"%-20s: %.2f%%%n\", \"Weighted Avg Rate\", avgRate * 100);\n```\n\n## Example 10: Custom Trade Info\n\n```java\n// Create tranche trade with detailed trade information\n\nTradeInfo detailedInfo = TradeInfo.builder()\n    .tradeDate(LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 15))\n    .settlementDate(LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 18))\n    .counterparty(StandardId.of(\"CPTY\", \"JP MORGAN\"))\n    .instrument(StandardId.of(\"ISIN\", \"US123456789\"))\n    .venue(StandardId.of(\"EXCH\", \"OTC\"))\n    .convention(StandardId.of(\"CONVENTION\", \"CDX-HY\"))\n    .putAttribute(\"strategy\", \"hedge\")\n    .putAttribute(\"client\", \"ACME Corp\")\n    .build();\n\nCdsTrancheTrade strategyTrade = CdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n    .info(detailedInfo)\n    .product(equityTranche)\n    .upfrontFee(AdjustablePayment.of(\n        CurrencyAmount.of(Currency.USD, 250_000),\n        LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 18)\n    ))\n    .build();\n\n// Access trade attributes later\nString strategy = strategyTrade.getInfo().getAttribute(\"strategy\").get();\nSystem.out.println(\"Trade strategy: \" + strategy);  // Output: hedge\n```\n\n## Key Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Builder Construction\nAlways use builder for creating products and trades:\n```java\nCdsTranche tranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n    .buySell(BuySell.BUY)\n    .underlyingIndex(index)\n    .attachmentPoint(0.03)\n    .detachmentPoint(0.07)\n    // ... complete all required fields\n    .build();\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Lazy Resolution\nResolve trades only when needed (expensive operation):\n```java\nCdsTrancheTrade trade = ...;  // Unresolved\n\n// Later, when pricing is needed:\nResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\nCurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(...);\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Market Data Injection\nUse dependency injection for rates provider:\n```java\nCreditRatesProvider ratesProvider = ...;  // Injected\nCurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(resolved, ratesProvider, valuationDate);\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Immutability\nProducts and trades are immutable - create new ones for modifications:\n```java\n// ❌ WRONG:\ntrade.setNotional(200_000_000);\n\n// ✅ RIGHT:\nCdsTrancheTrade modifiedTrade = CdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n    .info(trade.getInfo())\n    .product(CdsTranche.builder()\n        .from(trade.getProduct())\n        .notional(200_000_000)\n        .build())\n    .upfrontFee(trade.getUpfrontFee().orElse(null))\n    .build();\n```\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n- **Reuse Resolved Forms**: Don't resolve the same trade multiple times\n- **Parallel Pricing**: Use parallel streams for portfolios\n- **Curve Caching**: Cache credit curves across multiple pricings\n- **Batch Calculations**: Use calc engine for scenario analysis\n\n## Error Handling\n\n```java\ntry {\n    CdsTranche tranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n        .attachmentPoint(-0.01)  // INVALID\n        .detachmentPoint(0.05)\n        // ... other fields\n        .build();\n} catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n    System.out.println(\"Invalid tranche: \" + e.getMessage());\n    // Output: Invalid tranche: attachmentPoint must be >= 0\n}\n```\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe CdsTranche implementation provides comprehensive support for CDO tranche pricing and risk analysis within OpenGamma Strata, enabling quantitative analysis of structured credit .paymentSchedule(index.getPaymentSchedule())\n    .build();\n\n// Create senior tranche [7%-30%]\nCdsTranche seniorTranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n    .buySell(BuySell.BUY)\n    .underlyingIndex(index)\n    .attachmentPoint(0.07)       // 7%\n    .detachmentPoint(0.30)       // 30%\n    .currency(Currency.USD)\n    .notional(920_000_000.0)     // $920M notional for tranche\n PV=$%,12.0f%n\",\n        name, notional, rate * 100, pv.getAmount());\n}\n\ndouble portfolioPrice = totalPv / totalNotional;\ndouble avgRate = weightedRate / totalNotional;\n\nSystem.out.printf(\"%n%-20s: $%,12.0f%n\", \"Total Notional\", totalNotional);\nSystem.out.printf(\"%-20s: $%,12.0f%n\", \"Total PV\", totalPv);\nSystem.out.printf(\"%-20s: %.2f%%%n\", \"Portfolio Price\", portfolioPrice * 100);\nSystem.out.printf(\"%-20s: %.2f%%%n\", \"Weighted Avg Rate\", avgRate * 100);\n```\n\n## Example 10: Custom Trade Info\n\n```java\n// Create tranche trade with detailed trade information\n\nTradeInfo detailedInfo = TradeInfo.builder()\n    .tradeDate(LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 15))\n    .settlementDate(LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 18))\n    .counterparty(StandardId.of(\"CPTY\", \"JP MORGAN\"))\n    .instrument(StandardId.of(\"ISIN\", \"US123456789\"))\n    .venue(StandardId.of(\"EXCH\", \"OTC\"))\n    .convention(StandardId.of(\"CONVENTION\", \"CDX-HY\"))\n    .putAttribute(\"strategy\", \"hedge\")\n    .putAttribute(\"client\", \"ACME Corp\")\n    .build();\n\nCdsTrancheTrade strategyTrade = CdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n    .info(detailedInfo)\n    .product(equityTranche)\n    .upfrontFee(AdjustablePayment.of(\n        CurrencyAmount.of(Currency.USD, 250_000),\n        LocalDate.of(2024, 1, 18)\n    ))\n    .build();\n\n// Access trade attributes later\nString strategy = strategyTrade.getInfo().getAttribute(\"strategy\").get();\nSystem.out.println(\"Trade strategy: \" + strategy);  // Output: hedge\n```\n\n## Key Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Builder Construction\nAlways use builder for creating products and trades:\n```java\nCdsTranche tranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n    .buySell(BuySell.BUY)\n    .underlyingIndex(index)\n    .attachmentPoint(0.03)\n    .detachmentPoint(0.07)\n    // ... complete all required fields\n    .build();\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Lazy Resolution\nResolve trades only when needed (expensive operation):\n```java\nCdsTrancheTrade trade = ...;  // Unresolved\n\n// Later, when pricing is needed:\nResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\nCurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(...);\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Market Data Injection\nUse dependency injection for rates provider:\n```java\nCreditRatesProvider ratesProvider = ...;  // Injected\nCurrencyAmount pv = pricer.presentValue(resolved, ratesProvider, valuationDate);\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Immutability\nProducts and trades are immutable - create new ones for modifications:\n```java\n// ❌ WRONG:\ntrade.setNotional(200_000_000);\n\n// ✅ RIGHT:\nCdsTrancheTrade modifiedTrade = CdsTrancheTrade.builder()\n    .info(trade.getInfo())\n    .product(CdsTranche.builder()\n        .from(trade.getProduct())\n        .notional(200_000_000)\n        .build())\n    .upfrontFee(trade.getUpfrontFee().orElse(null))\n    .build();\n```\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n- **Reuse Resolved Forms**: Don't resolve the same trade multiple times\n- **Parallel Pricing**: Use parallel streams for portfolios\n- **Curve Caching**: Cache credit curves across multiple pricings\n- **Batch Calculations**: Use calc engine for scenario analysis\n\n## Error Handling\n\n```java\ntry {\n    CdsTranche tranche = CdsTranche.builder()\n        .attachmentPoint(-0.01)  // INVALID\n        .detachmentPoint(0.05)\n        // ... other fields\n        .build();\n} catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n    System.out.println(\"Invalid tranche: \" + e.getMessage());\n    // Output: Invalid tranche: attachmentPoint must be >= 0\n}\n```\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe CdsTranche implementation provides comprehensive support for CDO tranche pricing and risk analysis within OpenGamma Strata, enabling quantitative analysis of structured credit products.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

(Index PV @ Attachment)\n             × (Detachment - Attachment)\n             × Tranche Notional / Index Notional\n```\n\n### Tranches in Practice (CDX HY)\n- **Equity** [0%-3%]: Highest risk, highest coupon\n- **Mezzanine** [3%-7%]: Medium risk, medium coupon\n- **Senior** [7%-15%]: Lower risk, lower coupon\n- **Super-Senior** [15%-30%]: Lowest risk, lowest coupon\n\n---\n\n## 🔗 Relationship to Existing Code\n\n### Depends On (Must Exist)\n- CdsIndex, CdsTrade, ResolvedCds, ResolvedCdsIndex\n- IsdaCdsProductPricer, IsdaHomogenousCdsIndexProductPricer\n- CreditRatesProvider, CreditCouponPaymentPeriod\n- Strata core product and calc framework\n\n### Depended On By (Will Use This)\n- Portfolio analytics tools\n- Risk reporting systems\n- Structured credit analytics\n- CDO pricing and management systems\n\n---\n\n## 📚 References to Existing Code\n\nStudy these files while implementing:\n- **`CdsIndex.java`**: Product pattern (what to copy)\n- **`CdsIndexTrade.java`**: Trade pattern (what to copy)\n- **`ResolvedCdsIndex.java`**: Resolved product pattern (what to copy)\n- **`IsdaCdsProductPricer.java`**: Pricer pattern (understand delegation)\n- **`CdsIndexTradeCalculationFunction.java`**: Calc function pattern (what to copy)\n\n---\n\n## ⚠️ Common Pitfalls to Avoid\n\n1. **Not using Joda-Beans correctly**\n   - All fields must be `private final`\n   - All must have `@PropertyDefinition`\n   - Class must have `@BeanDefinition`\n\n2. **Forgetting defaults**\n   - Add `@ImmutableDefaults` method for default values\n   - Add `@ImmutablePreBuild` for pre-build processing\n\n3. **Circular dependencies**\n   - ResolvedCdsTranche shouldn't reference CdsTranche\n   - Only forward references allowed\n\n4. **Incomplete meta-bean implementation**\n   - Don't hand-write hash codes or equals methods\n   - Don't hand-write builder methods\n   - All generated by Joda-Beans\n\n5. **Missing validation**\n   - Validate attachment < detachment\n   - Validate both in range [0, 1]\n   - Use ArgChecker utilities\n\n---\n\n## 🤝 Getting Help\n\n### If you have questions about:\n\n| Question | See Document |\n|----------|--------------|\n| What is being built? | SUMMARY.md |\n| How should I implement this? | implementation_guide.md |\n| What does this class do? | architecture_overview.md |\n| How do I use this? | usage_examples.md |\n| Why is it designed this way? | solution.md |\n| What's the exact code structure? | cds_tranche_complete_implementation.md |\n\n---\n\n## 📝 Implementation Checklist\n\n### Planning Phase\n- [ ] Read SUMMARY.md\n- [ ] Review architecture_overview.md\n- [ ] Understand loss allocation semantics\n- [ ] Identify team members and roles\n\n### Implementation Phase - (Index PV @ Attachment)\n             × (Detachment - Attachment)\n             × Tranche Notional / Index Notional\n```\n\n### Tranches in Practice (CDX HY)\n- **Equity** [0%-3%]: Highest risk, highest coupon\n- **Mezzanine** [3%-7%]: Medium risk, medium coupon\n- **Senior** [7%-15%]: Lower risk, lower coupon\n- **Super-Senior** [15%-30%]: Lowest risk, lowest coupon\n\n---\n\n## 🔗 Relationship to Existing Code\n\n### Depends On (Must Exist)\n- CdsIndex, CdsTrade, ResolvedCds, ResolvedCdsIndex\n- IsdaCdsProductPricer, IsdaHomogenousCdsIndexProductPricer\n- CreditRatesProvider, CreditCouponPaymentPeriod\n- Strata core product and calc framework\n\n### Depended On By (Will Use This)\n- Portfolio analytics tools\n- Risk reporting systems\n- Structured credit analytics\n- CDO pricing and management systems\n\n---\n\n## 📚 References to Existing Code\n\nStudy these files while implementing:\n- **`CdsIndex.java`**: Product pattern (what to copy)\n- **`CdsIndexTrade.java`**: Trade pattern (what to copy)\n- **`ResolvedCdsIndex.java`**: Resolved product pattern (what to copy)\n- **`IsdaCdsProductPricer.java`**: Pricer pattern (understand delegation)\n- **`CdsIndexTradeCalculationFunction.java`**: Calc function pattern (what to copy)\n\n---\n\n## ⚠️ Common Pitfalls to Avoid\n\n1. **Not using Joda-Beans correctly**\n   - All fields must be `private final`\n   - All must have `@PropertyDefinition`\n   - Class must have `@BeanDefinition`\n\n2. **Forgetting defaults**\n   - Add `@ImmutableDefaults` method for default values\n   - Add `@ImmutablePreBuild` for pre-build processing\n\n3. **Circular dependencies**\n   - ResolvedCdsTranche shouldn't reference CdsTranche\n   - Only forward references allowed\n\n4. **Incomplete meta-bean implementation**\n   - Don't hand-write hash codes or equals methods\n   - Don't hand-write builder methods\n   - All generated by Joda-Beans\n\n5. **Missing validation**\n   - Validate attachment < detachment\n   - Validate both in range [0, 1]\n   - Use ArgChecker utilities\n\n---\n\n## 🤝 Getting Help\n\n### If you have questions about:\n\n| Question | See Document |\n|----------|--------------|\n| What is being built? | SUMMARY.md |\n| How should I implement this? | implementation_guide.md |\n| What does this class do? | architecture_overview.md |\n| How do I use this? | usage_examples.md |\n| Why is it designed this way? | solution.md |\n| What's the exact code structure? | cds_tranche_complete_implementation.md |\n\n---\n\n## 📝 Implementation Checklist\n\n### Planning Phase\n- [ ] Read SUMMARY.md\n- [ ] Review architecture_overview.md\n- [ ] Understand loss allocation semantics\n- [ ] Identify team members and roles\n\n### Implementation Phase -
